msg:Facilities: relatively new, the texture is good to the naked eye. The cushions on the seats against the wall in the lounge are not very ergonomic. You will feel tired if you lean against them, so you can only sit upright. There is no water retaining stone in the bathroom, and the water cannot be directly directed into the sink, which will make the floor mat very wet, which is a very low-level mistake.
Hygiene: No problem, the cleaning is very thorough the next day.
Environment: quiet in the bustling, the interior is well greened, and the exterior is not noisy at night.
Service: The check-in or out service is fast and clear, but the doorman and the service staff who handle the takeaway and rent umbrellas will be slack, and you can only wait there.
Minibar courtesy: a bit shabby for the hotel positioning.
Andaz Lounge designated beverage courtesy: The bar menu has options such as spirits, red wine, and dry white wine, and I was told that they are all self-service. But when ordering spirits, the waiter will take out another wine list and tell you that it is a chargeable item and needs to be purchased extra, which is very embarrassing.
Happy hour courtesy: average, but not bad.

The coffee bar in the room is an independent cabinet in South Asian style. The inner side of the window uses a translucent sliding partition to separate the fireworks of the city.
The service is very thoughtful. We felt that the hotel umbrella was too heavy when we went out on a rainy day, so the staff at the first floor outer door service desk lent us their own umbrella. The attitude of the front desk and staff everywhere was warm and decent. The room was carefully folded and the clothes were carefully folded. When leaving, the staff would take the initiative to ask, and there was no need to worry about moving boxes and delivering cars. Thank you!

msg:The title of the most beautiful hotel during this trip to Xiamen must be awarded to this Xiamen Andaz, which is different from the "old" Shanghai Andaz, this Xiamen Andaz is a proper "little fresh meat" of the Hyatt series. Opened in 2020, the interior is well maintained. The unique design of the Nanyang-style villa in the city is really outstanding. The outdoor public pool area gives people a feeling of vacationing in Singapore. People who like to take pictures may spend a day in this hotel . The location is also invincible, close to the train station, next to the Vientiane City, easy to eat and drink, easy to go anywhere.

The day before check-in, the hotel manager called to ask about the arrival time the next day, and said that the room would be arranged according to my preference, and the room would be ready when I arrived at noon. After check-in, the waiter will personally send you into the room, and will introduce you to the hotel's facilities and happy hour along the way. The service is very nice.

I booked a room with a view. To be honest, I can't see the difference from the big bed room? Because there is a high-rise building outside the window, and the construction site can be seen on the left side, in fact there is no landscape to speak of, maybe it's just that the floor is slightly better than the basic house. The overall design of the indoor public area is not as good as the public area, but overall the experience is good. I can give it four stars. The noise of the air conditioner is the lightest among all the hotels I have stayed in Xiamen. It is worthy of praise. You can sit on the stool for changing slippers as soon as you enter the door The design is also very user-friendly, the texture of the bathrobe is also very comfortable, and there is also an independent dressing table designed for girls, I like it.

The biggest highlight of this Andaz is that all guests can enjoy the happy hour of the hotel. In the afternoon, they can enjoy free coffee and other drinks (you still have to pay for desserts yourself). Because of YQ, the happy hour in the evening is changed to the bar on the L floor of the hotel. There are wine and snacks here, but there are not many types, and most of them are cold food. The mini bar in the guest room is free. Coke, coconut water, sparkling water, and Xiamen special snacks are all available, which is still very a**ospheric. In addition, the welcome fruit and mung bean cake provided by the room, it is completely unbearable to take it back to Shanghai.

The most important thing that cannot be missed in Hyatt hotels is catering. This Andaz‚Äôs breakfast provides semi-self-service a la carte service. You can eat famous Fujian cuisine flat food, sand tea noodles, etc., as well as Western-style eggs Benedict and French toast. , the products are exquisite and delicious, even the tea and coffee products provided are better than those produced by ordinary five-star hotels, which is remarkable. I also ate lunch at the hotel when I checked out the next day. The roast duck in the Chinese restaurant was still excellent as always. Never disappoints.

After talking about the advantages, I still have to talk about the disadvantages. The laundry products have been downgraded, LE LABO is gone, and they have been replaced with AZZI GLASSER. The choice of bedding is generally hard, and it is not as good as the ones selected by Hilton Curio for sleeping. The dressing table here There will be a creaking sound when you walk on the floor. Before going to bed at night, you have to pray that the residents upstairs don't go there in the middle of the night, otherwise the downstairs will hear it clearly.

Maybe next time I come to Xiamen, I won't stay here. I just need to experience it. At this price, I always feel that there is still room for improvement.
